









Dear Young Man,

Don’t Be the Simp Who Saves Her From Her Own Chaos



Let me paint you a picture. She’s over 30, worn out from years of reckless living, and now scrambling to reset her life. Her body count rivals the population of a small town, and her character is non-existent. She’s self-centered, manipulative, and thrives on drama. Financially, she’s a disaster—broke, directionless, yet entitled enough to believe she deserves a good, rich, responsible young man to marry. And here’s the kicker: after wasting her prime years on meaningless flings and chasing chaos, she’s now looking for a bailout.

Men, don’t be that guy. Don’t fall into the trap of believing it’s your duty to “rescue” her. You’ve worked too hard, sacrificed too much, and built your life from the ground up. She isn’t looking for love; she’s looking for a retirement plan. Let me break it down for you so you can see this charade for what it really is.

First, her past choices define her present reality. For years, she prioritized the fast life—ignoring discipline, responsibility, and self-respect. She chose men who treated her like a disposable commodity, and she reveled in the thrill of living without consequences. Now, the results of those choices have caught up with her. But instead of taking accountability, she wants you, the man who has spent years grinding and sacrificing, to clean up her mess. That’s not love or partnership—it’s opportunism.

Second, bad character doesn’t magically improve with age. A woman who’s spent her life being selfish, irresponsible, and combative won’t suddenly transform into a supportive partner because she’s desperate. Toxicity doesn’t fade—it evolves. The same manipulation, drama, and chaos she brought into every past relationship will poison your peace and your home. She’s not looking to build with you; she’s looking to leech off your stability. Don’t mistake her desperation for genuine change.

Third, entitlement is a massive red flag. She’s broke but acts like the world owes her something. She expects you to swoop in and save her, not because she’s earned your effort, but because she believes she’s entitled to it. That entitlement will bleed into every aspect of your relationship. No matter how much you give, it will never be enough. She’ll always want more—your money, your time, your emotional labor—while contributing nothing of value.

And let’s address the elephant in the room: a high body count comes with heavy baggage. This isn’t about morality; it’s about patterns. A woman who has treated relationships as disposable isn’t equipped to value real commitment. Her past is a map of her priorities, and those priorities didn’t include building anything meaningful. That baggage doesn’t just vanish. It becomes your problem the moment you let her into your life.

Make no mistake—she doesn’t want you. She wants what you can provide. Stability. Resources. A sense of security she could never create on her own. You’re not her partner; you’re her escape plan. After years of poor choices, she sees you as her lifeline. And the second things get tough, inconvenient, or less exciting, she’ll discard you like she has every other man before you.

Good, rich, responsible men don’t owe anyone a bailout. You’ve spent your life building yourself into a man of value. Don’t let guilt, manipulation, or lust make you forget your worth. You’re not obligated to sacrifice your peace, your resources, or your future for someone who didn’t value her own life until it was too late.

Instead, prioritize your standards and stick to them. Don’t settle for less just because society, your family, or even your loneliness pressures you to. A woman with discipline, ambition, and character will respect and build with you—not leech off you. Stay focused on your goals and keep your purpose at the forefront of your life. Your mission comes first, and no one has the right to derail it.

Learn to walk away. Strength isn’t just about what you can build; it’s about knowing when to say “no” to what doesn’t serve you. Protect your peace, your time, and your legacy.

At the end of the day, men, your value doesn’t lie in being someone’s safety net. You’ve worked too hard to become the man you are. Don’t throw it all away for someone who spent years living recklessly, only to now expect you to clean up the mess. Be sharp. Be wise. And most importantly, don’t be the unfortunate simp who sacrifices his empire for someone who never cared to build her own.

Stay wise..

Aklahyel Goni See less

Aivis Vasiļevskis
Par Timmu.
Esiet sveicināti, mīļie draugi. Šodienas ieraksts ir veltīts mazliet skumjām pārdomām par to, kas notiek ar mums, ar cilvēkiem, ar tā saucamo 'sabiedrību'.
Kā zināms, tad šodien parādījās sēru vēsts par to, ka Maskavā acīmredzot pašnāvību izdarījis kādreizējais LV basketbola izlases spēlētājs Jānis Timma. Tikai 32 gadu vecumā un ar potenciālu turpināt karjeru vēl gadiem. Kāds tam īsti ir iemesls, kāda bija viņa personiskā traģēdija - apmēram to var nojaust no soctīklu ierakstiem un kopējā dzīves stāsta, bet šajā gadījumā svarīgāks ir kas cits.
Tagad katrs medijs publicē šo ziņu un izsaka līdzjūtību. Taču vēl tikai pirms mēneša tie bija pilni ar ķengu rakstiem par Jāņa izvēli spēlēt Krievijā. Kas tikai viņš nebija dažādu 'eksperdu' slēdzienos - nodevējs, jukušais, neprātis, slims un kas tik ne. Uz mūžiem nolādēts un izslēgts no izlases utt.
Katrs šīs slimās 'sabiedrības'  loceklis varēja atkal izpausties pēc pilnas programmas, zākāties un lamāt cilvēku, kas viņam neko nav sliktu izdarījis, kas ir pārstāvējis šo valsti sportā un tad gan bija pietiekoši labs un vajadzīgs.
Tagad daudzi no tiem lej savas krokodila asaras, taču patieso dabu noslēpt ar to nevar. Patiesu līdzjūtību Jānim var izteikt tikai tie, kas atbalstīja viņu visā, gan LV izlasē, gan Krievijas klubā, nevis divkosīgi izvēlas tikai sev patīkamo. 
Šis notikums skaudri parāda to, ka lielākās 'sabiedrības' daļas īstenais 'latviskums' ir tieši šāds - akls naids, vienaldzība un divkosība. Varam karot ar tautībām, uzspiest vienīgo valodu, zāģēt pieminekļus un visā vainot 'padomju mantojumu', bet realitāte ir tajā, ka nekādas varas, iekārtas un laiks nav spējis mainīt to, kas šī 'sabiedrība' īsti ir. Ka visi šie 'eksperdi' un 'viedokļa paudēji' un mediji, kas to visu uzpūta teju kā nacionālu nodevību, ir ļoti lielā mērā vainojami cilvēka nāvē. Tā mēs atbalstam savējos? Tad paldies, ar šādiem draugiem ienaidniekus nevajag.
Neviens to negribēs atzīt, bet tā ir. Tik svarīgi bija atkal sajaukt kopā savus politiskās propagandas naratīvus un pasludināt kādu par vainīgu, lai kārtējo reizi piesegtu savu stulbumu, korumpētību un melus. Tam bija veltīti veseli raidījumi un studijas. Tika uzstrādāts vesels naida vilnis, ko cilvēks vienkārši nespēj izturēt. Tam nez no kurienes atradās nauda, resursi, tajā ieguldījās visi. Lai cilvēku likvidētu, nevis izprastu un atbalstītu. Kurš tagad gribēs pārstāvēt valsti, nest karogu, būt patriots? Pēc visa šī?  Laikam tikai morāli kropļi. 
Kā to Merķelis reiz par latviešiem aprakstīja, tā viss arī paliek spēkā. Varam klāt pievienot vēl nupat izskanējušo Akropoles Pringles kaudzes izgrābšanu un redzam, ka arī nekad briesmīgos padomju laikus nepieredzējusī jaunā paaudze ir tikpat naska "rietumu vērtībās" Tur ASV lielveikalu iznešana dienas laikā sen ir absolūti ierasta parādība.
Nezinu, vai šis notikums kaut kādā veidā satricinās šo naidpilno 'sabiedrību', vai mediji beigs kurināt naidu un melot. Droši vien, ka nē, jo šīs lietas tāpat saprot tikai tie, kam tāda sirdsapziņa vispār ir.  Acīmredzot, ka medijos notiek rūpīga atlase un tur strādā tikai tie, kam tādas nav.
Šobrīd Jānis ir labākā vietā par šo. Mēs pārējie varam tikai kārtējo reizi piefiksēt un mācīties. 
Spēja pielāgoties slimai sabiedrībai nav veselības mērs. /Krišnamurti/

@AaronSiriSG

Pfizer board member, @ScottGottliebMD, you look foolish attacking 
@RobertKennedyJr
 on CNBC (links to clips below) because it’s clear you lack basic knowledge regarding vaccines. For example:

     --Your claim that in “early 2000s … FDA reformulate[d] the existing MMR vaccine to take some of the preservatives out,” is false. Never happened. You are likely thinking about the removal of thimerosal in the early 2000s from various vaccines but as even CDC explains, “Measles, mumps, and rubella (MMR) vaccines do not and never did contain thimerosal.” https://cdc.gov/vaccine-safety/about/thimerosal.html…

     --Your claim that a child “can’t get vaccinated [for MMR] until age 2” is simply false. MMR is routinely given at one year of age and sometimes even earlier. https://cdc.gov/vaccines/hcp/imz-schedules/index.html…

     --Your claims regarding pertussis vaccines nonsensically ignore the fact that these products do not prevent transmission of the pertussis bacteria – they only provide, at best, personal protection. As a recent consensus paper of industry pertussis vaccine “experts” explained, “aPVs [pertussis vaccine] … cannot avoid infection and transmission. … aPV pertussis vaccines do not prevent colonization. Consequently, they do not reduce the circulation of B. pertussis and do not exert any herd immunity effect.” https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/31333640/

     --Your claims regarding polio nonsensically ignore the fact that the last wild case of polio in the U.S. was in 1979 and that the only polio vaccine used in the U.S. for the last 24 years only provides, at best, personal protection and does not prevent transmission of the polio virus. As CDC explains: “IPV [inactivated polio vaccine] … does not stop transmission of the virus.” https://cdc.gov/poliovirus-containment/diseaseandvirus/index.html…

     --You claimed that “we [Pfizer] don’t make the pediatric vaccines, Pfizer is not in that market” to deflect the claim that, as a board member of Pfizer, you have a serious conflict of interest in attacking RFK Jr. regarding pediatric vaccines. But, as you no doubt know, Pfizer does sell pediatric vaccines, including the Prevnar vaccine given to babies at 2, 4, 6, and 12 months of age, which was one of Pfizer’s top three selling products in 2023. https://pfizer.com/sites/default/files/investors/financial_reports/annual_reports/2023/Your… claim is either a lie or reveals deep ignorance.

     --Your claim regarding measles mortality is based on dubious and unreliable data and ignores the facts that (1) approximately 400 people total died annually in the U.S. in the years before the first measles vaccine in 1963 (amounting to around 1 death for every 500,000 Americans), and (2) mortality from measles declined by over 98% from 1900 to 1960 before the vaccine and was continuing to decline. https://stacks.cdc.gov/view/cdc/6200.  In any event, you dutifully ignore the fact that RFK Jr. has made clear he has no intention of taking away vaccines from anyone who wants them.

     --You claim RFK Jr. will cost lives, but I would argue that ignorance regarding vaccine products does and has cost lives. I welcome a public debate in which we can discuss the number of lives ignorance about vaccines has cost versus your speculations about those RFK Jr. will supposedly cause (a man who has actually devoted his life to saving the lives of children).

Your knowledge regarding these products is only matched by your track record as a public “health” official. The plummeting decline in childhood health from the early 1980s (from less than 13% with chronic disease to now well over 50%) continued unabated while you were FDA commissioner. Respectfully, you lack authority or a track record, let alone basic knowledge, to speak on the subjects you address in this interview (let alone to discuss this topic with Senators to dissuade them from confirming RFK Jr.)

If you were being honest, you would reveal that your real concern, as a board member of Pfizer, is that Pfizer's golden gooses – Covid-19 vaccines, Prevnar vaccines, RSV vaccines, etc. – will have to face the reality of the devastating harms they have caused to families across America. Your interview stinks of self-interest. The time for selling out America's children so pharma and its leaders, like you, can line their pockets has come to an end.

Ligijas meli par manīm ir bijuši ĻOTI graujoši, jo es kaut kādīgi ielaidu tik ļaunu dvēseli mūsu dzīvē. Mums visiem ir terapijas bijušas vajadzīgas — bet protams, ka neatbildētie jautājumi turpina graut ikdienu. 

Vai esam drošībā?

Ja kādreiz, Sandri, vēlies atklāt ko Tu par šiem pārkāpumiem zini, vai izlīgt ar mani, vari droši sazināties epastā. Mana epasta adrese ir dainis@dainis.net. Pēc “dainu meditācijām” laida tumšas, skaļas, binaurālās frekvences ar bērnu un dzīvnieku bļāvieniem — it kā viņus spīdzinātu. Ja tur notiek sātanisms, tad patiešām Tev iesaku no tās vides bēgt, un man arī dot ziņu. Ja citi bērni ir laupīti vai izmantoti — noteikti ziņo policijai uzreiz! 

Ar to, ka Tavi pousti FBā man dod ziņu par pasākumiem vietās un starp cilvēkiem, kur esam ar manu mazo mīļģimenīti piedzīvojušu izteikti graujošu ļaunumu - tagad atdraugošos no Tevīm. To nedaru ar dusmām — bet pašaizsardzībai. 

Patiešām ceru, ja kādreiz Tu nonāksi līdzīgā situācijā — ka Tev sniegs patiesu roku palīgā — un ka Tevi — kā mani šajā situācijā — neatstās novārtā. 







Sandri, Inese un Austris Kozuliņu pagrieza muguru Ligijas ļaunai uzvedībai pret mani un manu meitu. Ligija ir cilvēks bez kuras manas meitas laupīšana nebūtu varējusi notikt. Viņai vēl ir manas mantas -- viņa nav atbildējusi vai tīšām veicināja manas meitas laupīšanu -- un viņa nav ticami atbildējusi vai abortēja, zaudēja vai iztēloja mūsu bērniņu -- kam jau bijām izrunājuši vārdus. Šo Inese zin -- un nerīkojās tā, ka man sniegtu atbildes, uz kurām manai dvēselei patiešām ir pilnas tiesības. Inesei NAV TIESĪBAS dziedāt par mūsu tautas tikumību -- vienkārši vērojot to, ko Ligija izdarīja man un manai meitai -- un viņa vispāri no sākuma līdz beigām -- bija klāt. Viltīgi silti smaidi -- ĻAUNAS rīcības, ļaunas sirdis ļauna ietekme -- pēc kuras manai meitai vajadzēja 2+ gadus terapiju. Ļoti ceru, ka no šī koncerta izvairīsies ģimenes ar bērniem, un latvieši kuri dzīvo tikumīgu, godīgu, patiesu dzīvi

31
  · 
Joprojām internetā cilvēkiem iesaka vakcinēties un nebrīdina, ka vakcinācija veicina mirstību. 
Jāskaidro vēlreiz.
Vakcinācija augustā par trešdaļu palielināja, nevis samazināja vakcinēto mirstību no covid.
Tā nav viltus ziņa, par to liecina spkc grafiks, kurā attēlota nevakcinēto un vakcinēto mirstību augustā. [1]
Šāds grafiks tiek publiskots pirmo reizi, acīm redzot deputātu uzdotie jautājumi beidzot liek uzrādīt faktus.
Pirmajā stabiņā ir redzama nevakcinēto mirstība augustā, kas ir 1,9 uz 100 tūkstošiem nevakcinētu iedzīvotāju.
Otrajā stabiņā ir redzama daļēji vakcinētu cilvēku mirstība, kas ļauj salīdzināt mirstību vakcinēto un nevakcinēto cilvēku starpā. Ja vakcīna būtu droša, tad cilvēkiem, kas būtu saņēmuši vakcīnu, būtu jāmirst retāk, kā nevakcinētiem cilvēkiem. Daļēji vakcinēto cilvēku mirstība ir par trešdaļu lielāka, kā mirstība starp nevakcinētiem cilvēkiem. Tā ir 3 uz 100 tūkstošiem vakcīnu saņēmušo.  Stabiņā atspoguļotie fakti liecina, ka viena trešdaļa no tiem, kas vakcinējās un nomira no covid, būtu palikuši dzīvi, ja nebūtu vakcinējušies.
Šī iemesla dēļ, līdz tālākai faktu noskaidrošanai, vakcināciju ieteikt, nebrīdinot, ka tā par trešdaļu veicina vakcīnas saņēmēju mirstību, nav ētiski.
Trešajā stabiņā ir mirstība pilnīgi vakcinētiem cilvēkiem. Tā ir 0,4 uz 100 tūkstošiem pilnīgi vakcinētu cilvēku, kas ir mazāka kā nevakcinētiem un nepilnīgi vakcinētiem cilvēkiem. 
Ja kāds sola, ka vakcinācija mazinās mirstību no covid labāk kā nevakcinēšanās un kā pierādījumu norāda tikai pilnībā vakcinēto cilvēku mirstību, tad viņš izplata viltus ziņas. 
Mirstība starp pilnīgi vakcinētajiem neatspoguļo cilvēku mirstību pēc vakcīnas saņemšanas. Lai uzzinātu, kā vakcinācija ietekmē mirstību, pilnīgi vakcinēto mirstībai ir jāpieskaita arī daļēji vakcinēto mirstība, kas augustā bija augstāka kā nevakcinēto mirstība.
Ir jāsaprot, ka cilvēki, nemirst divreiz. Tie, kuriem vakcīna rada veselības traucējumus, vairums, acīm redzot, nomirst vēl nepilnīgi vakcinēti, tāpēc pilnīgi vakcinētie mirst mazāk uz to cilvēku rēķina, kas ir nomiruši nepilnīgi vakcinēti. Cilvēku mākslīgs dalījums nepilnīgi un pilnīgi vakcinētajos ir kļūdains, jo rada maldīgu priekšstatu par vakcīnu saņēmušo cilvēku mirstību. 
Apļveida diagrammā ir pieļauta augstāk minētā kļūda. Tur daļēji vakcinēto mirstība tiek pieskaitīta nevakcinēto mirstībai un salīdzināta ar pilnīgi vakcinēto mirstību. It kā tad, ja cilvēks nomirst līdz 14 dienām pēc vakcinācijas, viņš nebūtu saņēmis poti, kuru patiesībā ir saņēmis. Vakcinēto un pilnīgi vakcinēto mirstība ir jāskaita kopā, jo abas šīs grupas ir saņēmušas vakcīnu un tad jāsalīdzina ar nevakcinēto mirstību, kas ir kontrolgrupa, ja mēs gribam uzzināt kā vakcinācija iespaido mirstību un, vai vakcīna ir iesakāma. 
Augustā mirstība no covid starp nevakcinētajiem bija mazāka kā mirstība starp vakcinētajiem un nav publiskoti fakti par vakcinēto un nevakcinēto mirstību citos mēnešos. Turklāt, joprojām nav atklāta mirstība  no visiem veselības traucējumiem starp vakcīnu saņēmušajiem un nevakcinētajiem.
Tāpēc šobrīd ieteikt vakcināciju nav ētiski. Par vakcināciju var tikai informēt, brīdinot, ka ietekme uz kopējo mirstību nav zināma un augustā vakcinācija veicināja vakcīnu saņēmušo mirstību no covid.
[1] https://www.spkc.gov.lv/lv/covid-19-statistika...

Actually, it is science. I came from a background in science and nutrition. I realized that there was a variable (or two) that I hadn't accounted for, sunlight being one of them. Parts of our mitochondrion can run off sunlight, similar to plants. The mitochondrion was actually an invasive organism long ago in our system that became a symbiotic relationship forming the ADP->ATP cycle, but it can also use sunlight. (science has not told us the truth on this) Like Dr. Jubb, I have run for extended periods without any food, only tea and a bit of honey, gathering sunlight as energy, plus meditation. In the winter, I could not subsist only on sunlight because of where I live. I only needed to eat about 1/2 of my palm full of berries, and that was it, plus the sunlight, yoga, and meditation. I learned that when cleaned out, my skin became so absorbent that it pulled in water from the air, including nitrogen, and was able to actually form amino acids that, in school, I'd been told were impossible to do so because they required essential amino acids and could come from food only. (not true as I explored fasting) This isn't for everyone and should not be forced. I 'knew' and basically got a message along each part of the journey when I could live on various things... vegetarian, pescatarian, vegan, and eventually just fruits. Then I knew when I could do breathatarian. Do I live entirely without food now? No. I can though if I wish to and my system is completely detoxed/cleaned out. If someone forces this, it goes badly. I will also add that food is sometimes used by some in their spiritual journey to stay anchored and not leave their physical vessels turning into light bodies and wrapping up. This began to happen to me, and I realized that food (even meat) has the purpose of balancing us as we need to. Folks operating in lower frequency ranges are sustained by lower frequency foods better. Higher vibrations with higher vibrating foods, BUT I've also met some vegans and others that were way ungrounded and out of balance (top heavy in their chakras and energy systems) and needed to set vegan or higher vibration foods down for a bit to even things out. Sometimes folks are comfort eating/addiction eating. Sometimes people are eating foods to sustain themselves (which most of us need very little to do so actually). Sometimes those higher in vibration are eating food to stay anchored and not wrap up. To each their own and your mileage can and will vary. There is no rush. Don't force things.

Accountability For Health Industry Predators




Establish simple legal structures that define Health Industry Predation and hold perpetrators to account. 

Current examples are: 

* end of life care exploitation
* mandated medical experimentation
* coerced "well visits" where parents are threatened with the loss of their children 
* inappropriate diagnoses that lead to the use of inappropriate medications
* etc.

Instead of fining industries, the new laws would hold individuals to account along the entire production, marketing, and distribution chains practiced by Health Industry Predators. 

Health Industry Predation would be categorized as a type of organized criminal activity. 

When individuals and companies are charged and found guilty of Health Industry Predation, their businesses are shut down and their assets are seized. The foreseeable outcome of such a program would be billions if not trillions of dollars in cash on hand and assets being made available to build a HealthCare system that does not profit from predation.

Listen up, Men! 5 tricks a narcissistic women use to finish you. 
If you’re entangled with a narcissistic woman, know this: she’s mastered the art of manipulation. She’ll go to extreme lengths to impress strangers, putting on a flawless, charming act in public while treating you—the man she claims to love—with contempt behind closed doors. It’s a well-crafted game: she builds a shining public image so that if you ever speak up about her toxic behavior, others won’t believe you. They’ll see her as the perfect, kind, caring woman and question your perspective instead. This two-faced approach is designed to isolate you, making you feel trapped and questioning your own reality.
Narcissistic women use calculated, dangerous tactics to keep you confused, controlled, and emotionally drained. Here are five key strategies they use to manipulate you and protect their own image.
1. Love Bombing to Create Dependency
In the beginning, she’ll overwhelm you with affection, admiration, and attention. This phase is called love bombing, and it’s designed to make you feel like you’re the most important person in her world. She’ll shower you with compliments, spend as much time with you as possible, and make you believe she’s “the one.” This is a trap, meant to hook you emotionally and create a deep sense of dependency. Once you’re fully invested, the love bombing stops, and the real game begins. Robert Greene’s “The Art of Seduction” details how manipulators use charm as a weapon, hooking you only to later reveal their true intentions.
2. Gaslighting to Distort Your Reality
One of the most insidious tactics narcissists use is gaslighting. She’ll twist conversations, deny things she’s said or done, and make you doubt your memory and perception. She may say something hurtful, then deny it happened when you confront her, making you question your sanity. The goal is to destabilize you mentally, so you start doubting your own judgment. In “The 48 Laws of Power,” Robert Greene discusses how controlling someone’s perception is one of the strongest forms of manipulation. By distorting your reality, she weakens your confidence and makes you more controllable.
3. Triangulation to Create Jealousy and Self-Doubt
Narcissistic women will often bring a third party into the mix to make you feel insecure and keep you off balance. This is known as triangulation. She may casually mention how much another man respects or admires her, or she might subtly flirt in front of you, making you feel inadequate. This tactic serves two purposes: it boosts her ego and keeps you feeling insecure. By constantly comparing you to others, she undermines your self-worth and keeps you chasing her approval. Triangulation is a classic tactic to create jealousy, control, and emotional chaos.
4. Playing the Victim to Manipulate Sympathy
When a narcissistic woman gets called out or faces conflict, she’ll often play the victim card, making it seem as though she’s the one suffering. She may cry, act hurt, or claim that you’re mistreating her—all while ignoring her own toxic behavior. This tactic is meant to manipulate sympathy, both from you and from others. By casting herself as the victim, she makes you feel guilty and responsible, keeping you locked in the relationship out of obligation. In “The 48 Laws of Power,” Greene warns of those who manipulate others through sympathy, turning vulnerability into a weapon.
5. Constantly Shifting the Blame to Keep You on the Defensive
A narcissistic woman will rarely, if ever, take responsibility for her actions. Instead, she’ll constantly shift the blame back onto you, making you feel like you’re always at fault. If you bring up her hurtful behavior, she’ll deflect and point out your shortcomings, leaving you feeling guilty and questioning yourself. This tactic keeps you on the defensive, diverting attention away from her flaws and putting the burden on you. By keeping you in a constant state of self-doubt, she maintains control and avoids accountability. This shifting blame tactic is common among manipulators who avoid taking responsibility for their actions.
The Bottom Line
Dealing with a narcissistic woman is like playing a rigged game where every move you make seems to turn against you. She’ll use love bombing to hook you, gaslighting to control your perception, triangulation to keep you insecure, victimhood to manipulate sympathy, and blame-shifting to keep you on the defensive. If you find yourself constantly doubting your reality, questioning your worth, or feeling isolated, it’s a red flag you’re dealing with a narcissist.
To protect yourself, stay alert, recognize these tactics for what they are, and remember that you don’t have to endure emotional manipulation disguised as love. Set firm boundaries, protect your mental health, and be prepared to walk away if these toxic patterns persist. 	1	Korelācija pret kausalitāti (cēloņsakarību) Kausālā saistība starp Corynebacterium diphtheriae un difterijas slimību ir visai vāji pierādīta. Veselos cilvēkos var iztestēt diftēriju. Tātad izgudroja jēdzienu “nontoxigenic tox gene-bearing (NTTB) strains.” Vai asimptomātiski “nesēji” varbūt nepierāda ka šīs baktērijas ir pat mums labvēlīgas? Tiešām vajag stingrus, īstus, kārtīgus eksperimentus, nevis tukšas un vāji pierādītas teorijas. 
	2	Kocha postulāti Vai Kleba un Löflera pētījums 1883. gadā atbilst Koha postulātiem? Vai bija zinātnei vajadzīgās kontroles? Mūsdienu pētījumi nav atkārtojuši Kleba un Löflera atklājumus, un pats Pasteur-s esot apšaubījis mikrobu kausalitāti (itsevišķi savas mūžas pēdējos mēnešos).
	3	Pārspīlēta uzmanība mikrobiem Fokusējoties tikai uz Corynebacterium diphtheriae, tiek ignorēti vides faktori, piemēram, uzturs, vides piesārņojums un stress, kas ietekmē slimošanu. Šāda veida aklums var radīt nepareizu izpratni par difterijas etioloģiju.
	4	Vakcinācijas paradokss Vai difterijas vakcīnu panākumi sakrīt ar labāku sanitāriju, sabiedrisku higēnu un veselības aprūpi? Ko tas nozīmē par diftērijas slimošanas cēloņiem un vakcīnu pieņemto nepieciešamību? Ja citi faktori uzlaboja sabiedriskos slimības rādītājus, tad vai vakcīnu pārdošana nav tāda kā krāpniecība — ņemot citu faktoru veiksmi un viltīgi to aprakstot kā savu? Ilgtermiņa vakcinācijas veselības ietekme vispāri joprojām tiek pētīta.
	5	Vides teorijas ignorēšana Uz mikrobiem vērsta uzmanība ignorē Antoina Bešampa vides teoriju, kas uzsver, ka vides faktori būtiski ietekmē slimošanas gaitas un veselību, nevis tikai mikrobu klātbūtne.





	1	Correlation vs. Causation The link between Corynebacterium diphtheriae and diphtheria doesn't confirm causation. Asymptomatic carriers complicate its role in disease, necessitating rigorous experimental designs.
	2	Koch's Postulates Revisited Klebs and Loeffler's adherence to Koch's postulates in 1883 is questionable due to inadequate controls and criteria fulfillment. Modern studies have not consistently reproduced their findings, and Koch himself recognized limitations in his criteria. 
	3	Overemphasis on Microbe Focusing solely on Corynebacterium diphtheriae neglects environmental and host factors like nutrition and pollution that influence disease susceptibility. This oversimplification risks misunderstanding diphtheria's etiology.
	4	Vaccine Paradox The success of diphtheria vaccines coincides with better sanitation and healthcare, suggesting they may enhance immune function rather than solely neutralizing bacteria. Long-term health effects of vaccination are still under investigation. 
	5	Ignoring Terrain Theory The focus on microbes overlooks Antoine Béchamp's terrain theory, which emphasizes that environmental factors significantly influence disease susceptibility through cellular health rather than just microbial presence.



Correlation vs. Causation: While C. diphtheriae is often found in diphtheria cases, this doesn't necessarily prove causation.

were  Koch's Postulates: fulfilled by Klebs and Loeffler in 1883 — were there adequate controls — also have Koch’s postulates been fulfilled regarding diphtheriae to this day?

Overemphasis on Microbe: Focusing solely on C. diphtheriae ignores other potential contributing factors like nutritional deficiencies or environmental toxins [12].

Vaccine Paradox: The apparent success of vaccines isn’t scientifically valid and doesn't necessarily prove bacterial causation. The vaccine argument is an oversimplification: Reducing diphtheria to a single bacterial cause oversimplifies complex biological processes and ignores much more serious factors like hygiene and industrial toxins. 


Ignoring Terrain Theory: The focus on microbes ignores Antoine Béchamp's terrain theory, which suggests environmental factors play a crucial role in disease manifestation [

Dainis W. Michel
Ilze Kon sarakstā ir vīrietis pēc dzimuma, bet ne pēc rakstura. Pieņemt ņepieņemamo, ar atrunu "visi esam savādās attīstības stadijās," manuprāt neveicina sabiedrisko veselību.
Par piedošanu, daudzi ir nonākuši maldinošā miglā dēļ nepilnvērtīgas mūsu Tēvreizes tulkojumiem, un dēļ jaunezotēriķu kaitīgām filozofijām. Musturam: varmācība-piedošana, pārkāpums-piedošana, abjūss-piedošana, utt., mums, itsevišķi latviešiem, ir jāpieliek punkts. To dara ar: atbildību.
Vīrieša raksturā būtu jābūt patiesiskumam, un vīriešiem, lai būtu igtspējīga sabiedrība -- ir uz patiesības pamata -- jāspēj vienoties un viens otru, savējosm, sabiedrību un tautu -- pasargāt.
Blakus piedošanai ir "atdošana," un es atdodu, tiem, kas ir man un manai meitai un ģimenei darījuši pāri -- viņu doto. Tāda līmena traumatizējumus, varmācību, un pārkāpumus -- vienkārši atstāt -- un blakus stāvēt un neko nedarīt (tā var arī dažus citus "vīriešus" sarakstā aprakstīt), ir dziļi un sāpīgi nevīrišķīga uzvedība.
Sapratne mums dod iespēju tālredzīgi saskatīt, kā zināma veida uzvedība iespaidos mūsu tautu -- un diemžēl -- varam nevīrišķīgu, gļēvu, nepatiesu, melīgu un ļaunu uzvedību "saprast," bet tas nenozīmē, ka mums jāpiekrīt.
Par empātiju -- nu esmu tagad ilgus gadus centies aizstāvēt empātiju, gan sakarā ar medicīniskām cilvēktiesībām, gan ar dziļu empātiju pret citiem manu meitiņu audzinot -- gan izteikti empātiski uzvedoties sabiedrībā -- un vēl pat skaidrojot, kas vispāri empātiskā komunikācija ir (var lasīt Stephen Covey -- ļoti labi apraksta empātisko komunikāciju un tās vērtību). Jā -- ar NVC (nonviolent communication) un empātiju -- un empātisko komunikāciju -- var ļoti kritisakas situācijas risināt -- un iespējams izvilkt mūsu tautu no tās bedres, kurā esam nonākuši.
Bet cik ilgi vispirms mīļi komunicēt par empātiju, tad empātiski uzvesties un tikt izmantotam, tad skaļāk un formalizētāk izteikties par empātiju --- nu atkal tikt ignorētam un noraidītam -- vai tad lai nonākam līdz punktam, ka par guvumiem kurus empātija sabiedrībai sniedz -- jābļauj?
Ja ignorē, tagad 3 gadus, blakus stāvējoša vīrieša kritisko situāciju - lai gan viņš Tev ir talkojis, gatavojis, dziedājis, ir bijis pilnīgi ar mieru Tev sniegt roku palīgā - nu tad var secināt, ka šī sabiedrība ir lauzta.
Vismaz mazlietiņ palīdz "diftērijas" gadījumā nonākošo ģimeni -- bet diftērijas baktērijas nav pat pilnībā pierādītas kā kausālas ar simptomiem -- tas nozīmē -- var būt pozitīvs tests bez simptomiem.
Bet diemžēl, Latvijā valda ne tikai apātija pret savējiem -- bet burtiski naidīgi graujoša ļauna uzvedība pret viens otru.
Sarakstā ir vīrieši, kas būtu varējuši iestāties par patiesiskumu -- bet viņi atļāva man tikt melni apmelotam. Gadiem. Kur ir viņu vīrišķība?
Cik vienkārši būt pavaicāt manai meitai: vai bija kā sievieteX stāsta?
Cik vienkārši būtu bijis man palīdzēt kaut vai tikai atgūt manas mantas?
Nē, atļāva man tikt traumatizējoši apmelotam un izraidītam no visai plaša sabiedrības loka. Deva meliem un ļaunumam priekšroku un tas ir tik ļoti nevīrišķīgi, ka vēmiens nāk domājot, ka tieši šie "vīrieši" ir tie, kas pat vīrišķības seminārus Latvijā vada.
Ahā, tātad, ja vīrietim konkrēti būtu jāuzvedās kā vīrietiem (aizstāvēt patiesību, sargāt, vienoties spēkos un risināt situācijas, viens otram palīdzēt), teiksim ja ir praktiska, konkrēta vajadzība, piemēram: kad bērns tiek laupīts ar sievietesX līdzdalību -- tad vai ir OK, ja visus vīrīšķības principus pamet? Neko nedara? Nepalīdz, neiesaistās -- un vēl piedalās graujošā melu kampaņā pret patiešām nevainīgu vīrieti -- kas tāda veida melu kampaņu nekad nebija savā dzīvē pelnījis -- tas ir ok?
Tā ir tā pati enerģija ar kuru izsūtīju vai nodeva vai nošāva -- mūsu vecvecāku paaudzē. Vai tiešām tā ir "vīrišķīga" uzvedība -- otram vīrietim darīt pāri un teikt: pats pelnīja, pats piesauca, viņš izteicās pret valsti utt utt utt?



Ainārs, iespējams, ka es penzijas gados tuvāk intresēšos, bet sobrīd gan ne. Esot intresanti skatīties "emergency flight routes," jo tie vairāk rādot uz plakanās zemes modeli. Nu un?

Viens pozitīvs rezultāts, par manu visai seklo ieskati plakanzemju teorijās, ir ka mums daudz labāk derētu modelis ar 13 mēnešiem, tātad 13x28 ar to vienu "lieko" dienu...

Cilvēki arī rāda uz: "slit test," un domā, ka tas rāda uz modeli, ka dzīvojam virtuālā realitātē. Bet tā ir non-sequitur domkļūda -- kas tomēr pilnībā neapstrīd iespēju, ka dzīvojam virtuālā simulācijā. 

OK:

2) dzīvojam uz plakanas virsmas ar stikla pusbļodu virs mūsu galvām (bet tad jautājums paliek, kur vispāri tā plakanā sistēma atrodas -- vai tā vienkārši peld kaut kādā jūrā, un kur tā jūra tad atrodas, utt.) 
3) dzīvojam virtuālā realitātē
4) kaut kas cits

Teach While You Sleep
It sounds like you're looking for someone to 'publish' your offer Dainis. This is a super common thing where a marketer will take an expert (in this case, you) and run all their marketing and the expert will deliver any products and typically run a higher-ticket coaching program on the back end. Profit splits vary, but it's pretty common for the marketer to keep the front end profit (or loss since the marketer is typically the one putting up the cash to run ads to cold traffic) and there'll be a split of the back end coaching program. I know people who make a living publishing other people’s offers.
However, with your offer in its current state, you may find it difficult - maybe impossible - to find an experienced marketer willing to publish you. The reason I say that is because it's not 100% clear what your product does (the outcome a student will get from it) or who the product is for. At the moment, the messaging is about your method, not the students' outcome.
The sales page talks about being for 'professional music teachers', but also for people 'just starting out'. No single person reading the sales page will have a “Oh shit - this is EXACTLY what I need” kind of response because no single person is simultaneously a professional music teacher, but also just starting out.
The outcomes it promises look like they're quite far-ranging as well - from sight-singing to songwriting to improvising on instruments to more general music literacy. That’s not to say that your method can’t help people with all these things, but talking about ALL of them means the messaging gets very diluted.
For example, you also mention that the method is 'amazing' for guitar, but I'm still not 100% sure what outcome a guitarist will get from the core offer. That variation you shared about writing your songs down is clearer, but honestly, that doesn't seem like a problem that millions of people have - which is what you need for the kind of scale you talk about. It seems like a very specific problem that very few people have - which means needing to charge high prices, but this problem doesn't really seem like something that commands a high price. Most singer-songwriters don’t ever need to do this; they would usually just write the lyrics and chords down and can just record the melody demo as a voice memo on their phone. And if you’re talking about guitarists specifically, the thing that will likely go through their minds is "I can just use tablature to write down songs."
Another reason it might be tricky to find someone to publish you is that you also mention a $7 CPA, but if you're talking about running cold Facebook ads, that's unrealistically low; especially if you want to scale. Your CPAs will go up after you've addressed the most eager buyers in the market and with the total value of your funnel at the moment - even with a $97 upsell - the economics of running this at scale just don't work out. If you had a high ticket coaching program on the back end that cost thousands of dollars, then that would be a different story, but I don’t know what that would look like in your case.
You also mention your credentials and awards, but honestly, people don't care about that stuff; they care about what you can do for THEM. I also have degrees, but I almost NEVER mention them in my bass guitar business because it doesn't matter at all to the people watching my videos and going through my courses.
If you wanted this to be appealing to a marketer to publish, then I’d recommend making the messaging less confusing; less about your method and more about the outcome that a single type of student would get from learning what you teach. Try to make the core audience for the offer more on the beginner side (since mathematically, there will always be more beginners, and therefore, more potential to scale), make the total addressable market as large as possible, and increase the total value of the funnel so that there IS room to scale when CPAs rise to $50-$100+ if you start to seriously scale.
Also, marketers who publish experts will also usually prefer working with people who already have at least some kind of established audience as well - I'm not sure if that's something you already have, but if so, it would be appealing to a publisher.
All in all, this would likely be a hard sell to an experienced marketer, but from what you've written, it sounds like that’s what you want.

Vai jēdziens "desa" izsaka, kādas ir sastāvdaļas? Ā, "desā" ir "gaļa," nu ok - ko tas vispāri nozīmē: beigtas govs līķis ar sāli. Vai "gaļēdāji" saka: beigta zivs, govslīķis, samalti cūkas dibens muskuļi?

Tikai jo pašreizējā sabiedrībā, cilvēki manipulē ar ēdienu nosaukumiem, lai apslēptu, to ko ēd, un pārsvarā, "desās," ir paslēpti beigti dzīvnieki, nenozīmē, ka tie kas augu valsts uzturu ēd, nedrīkst "desās" salikt ko viņi paši vēlās. 

Ir desu formā ļoti veselīgi augu valsts ēdieni - un ir arī ļoti neveselīgi pārproducēti, plastmasai līdzīgi ēdieni. 

Esmu ēdis augu valsts uzturu apmēram 15 gadus. Dēļ sabiedriskās kritikas, atturos no jēdziena "vegāns." Veselības un citi guvumi ir bijuši ļoti, ļoti skaisti -- itsevišķi saskarsme ar savvaļas dzīvniekiem. 

Un taisu absurdi garšīgu vegānu jāņu sieru. 

Un to saucu par "sieru," jo es to drīkstu. 

Kamdēļ gaļēdāji domā, ka viņi drīkst atņemt tiem, kas ēd augu valsts uzturu, ēdienu formas nosaukumus?

Saliek plācenīti -- taisa burgeru. Nāk gaļēdāji un saka, kamdēļ Tu to sauc par "burgeru," burgeros taču ir jābūt beigtiem dzīvniekiem.

Google Search Operators List

Here is a complete list of all working Google advanced search operators:
	•	“search term” Use this to do an exact-match search.
	•	OR Search for this OR that. This will return results related to the two terms or both.
	•	AND Search for this AND that. This will only return results related to the two terms
	•	– Exclude a term or search phrase.
	•	* Acts as a wildcard and will match any word or phrase.
	•	( ) Groups multiple terms or operators to control how the search is shown.
	•	$ Search for prices.
	•	define: Displays the meaning of a word in a card-like result.
	•	Cache: Returns the most recent cached version of a web page (as long as the page is indexed).
	•	filetype: Shows results of a certain filetype (PDF, DOCX, TXT, PPT, etc.)
	•	site: Limit results to a specific website.
	•	related: Find sites related to another site.
	•	intitle: Find pages that contain a specific word in the title.
	•	allintitle: Like “intitle,” this finds web pages containing all of the specific words in the page title.
	•	inurl: Finds pages with a certain word in the URL.
	•	allinurl: Similar to “inurl,” this finds web pages containing all of the URL’s specific words.
	•	intext: Finds pages containing a specific word in the content.
	•	allintext: Finds results containing all of the specific words somewhere on the page.
	•	AROUND(X) This proximity search finds pages containing two words (or phrases) within X words of each other.
	•	weather: Finds the weather for a specific location.
	•	stocks: See stock information
	•	map: View map results for a location search.
	•	movie: Finds information about a specific movie.
	•	in Convert one unit into another (like currencies, weights, temperatures, etc.)
	•	source: Find news results from a certain source within Google News.

Sculpture "Teleport", monument to Grand Duke of Courland Jacob Kettler in central Kuldīga (Goldingen) in western Latvia. October 27, 2023

The sculpture ("Teleport") was created in 2013 by sculptor Gļebs Panteļejevs and architect Andris Veidemanis. The object has two sides, symbolically revealing different eras. The front side, made of polished aluminium castings, symbolises the 21st century, while the back side is meant to be 17th century, made of rusted cast iron.
The object, which is more than two metres high, depicts Duke Jacob coming from the past into the 21st century. The site was chosen for its symbolic significance, as it is here that Liepāja Street marks the end of the Old Town and the beginning of the new part of Kuldīga. The object has two sides, each representing a different time period. The rusted cast-iron casting facing the Old Town symbolises the time of the Duchy, while the one facing the Town Square is a futuristic aluminium casting, from which Jacob emerges in the 21st century.
The greatest Duke of the Duchy of Courland and Semigallia reigned from 1642 to 1682. Under the Grand Duke Jacob of the Kettler family, Courland reached the highest stage of its development and power. Under his rule, shipbuilding developed rapidly, the first manufactories appeared and agricultural production improved. The Duke managed to create a large fleet, whose ships carried to Western Europe cereals, meat, butter, wool, timber and everything else produced by his manufactories and the manors of Zemgale and Kurzeme. The fleet was large and powerful, sailing not only to Europe, but also to Tobago and Gambia, establishing colonies there and taking sugar, coffee and spices to Europe.
The principality built ships, produced paper and napkins, wove cloth, brocade and tapestries. Ironworking was developed, nails were hammered, anchors and bells were made, guns were cast and firearms made, vodka was made, vinegar was produced and gunpowder was ground in mills. Sailcloth, cordage and hemp rope were also produced. The Duke also thought about seed breeding, raised pedigree livestock, improved the land with land reclamation... He contributed to economic and cultural prosperity, created manufactures, developed shipbuilding and industry, crafts and trade, founded colonies in Gambia and Tobago.

Dear Maestro Zimmer,

Your remarkable ability to evoke profound emotions through music has transformed the cinematic landscape. From the haunting themes of The Lion King to the exhilarating scores of Inception and Dunkirk, your work resonates deeply with audiences, creating unforgettable experiences. As you once said, “I want to go and write music that announces to you that you can feel something” — a philosophy that aligns perfectly with our mission at Klavins Pianos.

Imagine the Klavins Model 450i in a dedicated performance space, serving as both a stunning architectural centerpiece and an instrument capable of delivering the rich, immersive sound that your compositions demand. Standing at 4.5 meters tall, the 450i offers an unparalleled acoustic experience, allowing you to explore new sonic dimensions and push the boundaries of your creativity.

Key Features of the Klavins 450i:
	•	Architectural Integration: Its striking design can be seamlessly incorporated into concert halls or studios, enhancing both the aesthetic and acoustic qualities of the space.
	•	Customized Design: We can tailor every aspect of the piano to reflect your artistic vision, ensuring it complements your unique sound.
	•	Unmatched Sound Quality: With strings measuring up to 3.9 meters in length, this piano produces a resonant tone that captures the emotional depth of your most powerful scores.
Your journey in film scoring exemplifies a commitment to innovation and emotional storytelling. As you noted, “If something happened where I couldn't write music anymore, it would kill me.” The Klavins 450i is designed for artists like you—those who live for their craft and seek instruments that inspire new creative possibilities.

In addition to the 450i, we also offer smaller models, such as the Una Corda Graffiti Line Piano. This model features customizable designs inspired by your iconic film scores and incorporates advanced sound manipulation techniques to further enhance your musical expression.

Maestro Zimmer, I believe that the Klavins 450i could serve as an extraordinary tool for your creative endeavors, inspiring new compositions and collaborations. I would love to discuss how we can help you realize this vision for your performance space.

Please feel free to reach out at +371 24 991 446 or dainis@klavins-pianos.com. I look forward to exploring this exciting opportunity with you.

In pursuit of sonic excellence,

Dainis W. Michel

Sea Eagle II, built by Royal Huisman, is an 81-meter (266 feet) three-masted schooner and is currently the largest aluminum sailing yacht in the world. Designed by Dykstra Naval Architects and Mark Whiteley, this yacht features a narrow and efficient hull, a Panamax rig, and advanced engineering that includes the world's largest carbon rudder. The yacht's displacement at full load is 1,050 tons, and it is equipped with powerful winches capable of an 18-tonne pulling load.
The yacht's design emphasizes both performance and luxury, with a sleek plumb bow, spacious deck areas, and a refined interior. It accommodates up to 12 guests in luxurious settings and offers amenities such as a cinema room, gym, sauna, and a variety of water sports equipment. The yacht's owner, Dr. Samuel Yin, a Taiwanese billionaire, uses the yacht for both business and leisure, reflecting his preference for elegant, high-performance vessels.

"Tik pacieties, debesīs labāki būs!"

Virs zemes nav laimes, tik zvēru pulks bļauj,
Viens otram iz mutes tie kumosu rauj,
Un priecīgs ikkatris, kad vēders tam pilns,
Kad bērni ir veseli, dzīvoklis silts.
Un glaimojot salkušie rakstnieki sauc:
"Cik praktiska tauta, tai cerību daudz!"

Jā, cerību gan. Bet nosirmos laiks,
Vēl redzams būs strādnieku moku pilns vaigs,
Vēl liekēži slinkos un godīgi krāps,
Vēl ļaudis pēc debesu valstības slāps,
Zem kājām varmākas taisnību mīs,
Par kaujamiem lopiem vēl cilvēkus dzīs,
Un muļķīgas dzejas vēl dzejnieki kals
Un vaimanās paši, kad salks tie un sals.

 Fear of Your Parents' Old Age 

"There  is a break in the family history, where the ages accumulate and  overlap, and the natural order makes no sense: it’s when the child  becomes the parent of their parent."
It’s when the father grows older and begins to move as if he were walking through fog. Slowly, slowly, imprecisely.
It’s when one of the parents who once held your hand firmly when you were little no longer wants to be alone.
It’s when the father, once strong and unbeatable, weakens and takes two breaths before rising from his seat.
It’s  when the father, who once commanded and ordered, now only sighs, only  groans, and searches for where the door and window are—every hallway now  feels distant.
It’s when one of the parents, once willing and hardworking, struggles to dress themselves and forgets to take their medication.
And we, as their children, will do nothing but accept that we are responsible for that life.
The life that gave birth to us depends on our life to die in peace.
Every child is the parent of their parent's death. Perhaps the old age of a father or mother is, curiously, the final pregnancy.
Our last lesson. An opportunity to return the care and love they gave us for decades.
And  just as we adapted our homes to care for our babies, blocking power  outlets and setting up playpens, we will now rearrange the furniture for  our parents.
The first  transformation happens in the bathroom. We will be the parents of our  parents, the ones who now install a grab bar in the shower.
The grab bar is emblematic. The grab bar is symbolic. The grab bar inaugurates the "unsteadiness of the waters."
Because the shower, simple and refreshing, now becomes a storm for the old feet of our protectors.
We cannot leave them for even a moment.
The  home of someone who cares for their parents will have grab bars along  the walls. And our arms will extend in the form of railings.
Aging  is walking while holding onto objects; aging is even climbing stairs  without steps. We will be strangers in our own homes. We will observe  every detail with fear and unfamiliarity, with doubt and concern.
We will be architects, designers, frustrated engineers. How did we not foresee that our parents would get sick and need us?
We will regret the sofas, the statues, and the spiral staircase. We will regret all the obstacles and the carpet.
Happy  is the child who becomes the parent of their parent before their death,  and unfortunate is the child who only appears at the funeral and  doesn't say goodbye a little each day.
My friend *Joseph Klein accompanied his father until his final moments.
In  the hospital, the nurse was maneuvering to move him from the bed to the  stretcher, trying to change the sheets when Joe shouted from his seat:  Let me help you. He gathered his strength and, for the first time, took  his father into his arms. He placed his father's face against his chest.
He  cradled his father, consumed by cancer: small, wrinkled, fragile,  trembling. He held him for a long time, the time equivalent to his  childhood, the time equivalent to his adolescence, a long time, an  endless time. By Your Side Nothing Hurts
Rocking his father back and forth. Caressing his father. Calming his father. And he said softly:

 I'm here, I'm here, Dad! "What a father wants to hear at the end of his life is that his child is there."
I love you, Dad, wherever you are, I always think of you, I will never forget you...

Other cultures are different from ours. 

South Korea
In South Korea, cat meat was historically brewed into a tonic as a folk remedy for neuralgia and arthritis, not commonly as food. Modern consumption is seen and more likely to be in the form of cat soup, though the number of people who consume cat soup is considered minimal, compared to a relatively popular dog meat.

Julien Dugnoille wrote in The Conversation that cat meat is mostly consumed by middle-aged working-class women for perceived health benefits, and that usually 10 cats are needed to produce a small bottle of cat, or goyangi, soju (an alcoholic elixir thought to keep arthritis at bay for a few weeks at a time).

According to In Defense of Animals, 100,000 cats are killed yearly to make cat soju in South Korea. Cats are not farmed for their meat in the country, so the trade involves ferals and strays. Nonetheless, the trade is mostly done underground, and the great majority of the population is not even aware that cat consumption exists in the country. Moreover, eating cat meat is highly stigmatized throughout the country, unlike eating dog meat, which is often criticized but not universally stigmatized.

https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cat_meat

#Negritude, African Literature and Language Choice#
Expectations:
1. What is negritude? How did it come about?
2. What is African Literature? What gave rise to this variety of World literature?
3. Language debate in African Literature; which language should Africans use in expressing their experience and their literary works?
(1) Negritude:
Negritude is a  cultural, political and literary movement that began around 1930, spread through, 40s, and gain extrem popularity in the  ’50s.
 At the out set, in the literary world, it began among French-speaking African and Caribbean writers living in Paris as a protest against French colonial rule and the policy of assimilation. Assimilation is a colonial policy, that aimed at transforming all Africans (particularly those in “French” colonies) by either luring or forcing them to integrate,  adapt and practice the way of life of the French people. It a policy that intended turning all Africans into black French men and women. To accomplish this goal, France had to eliminate all African cultures and assimilate all Africans into French culture. This policy never sat well with many Africans because it surpressed all the distinctive characteristics an Africans and this resulted to an intellectual protest.
 Negritude was majorly promoted by Léopold Sédar Senghor ( the first elected president of the Republic of Senegal in 1960) 
Some of the major principles of Negritude are: 
1. Celebration of Black culture and identity
2. Resistance to colonialism, racism, and oppression
3. Emphasis on the unique experiences and perspectives of Black people
4. Rejection of Eurocentric values and norms
5. Promotion of African and Caribbean cultures as equal to European cultures
In Literature, Negritude writers emphasized the following;
1. "Blackness" as a source of pride and strength
2. The importance of African and Caribbean heritage
3. The struggle for decolonization and independence
4. The role of literature and art in promoting social change
Major Contributors:
1. Léopold Sédar Senghor (Senegal)
2. Aimé Césaire (Martinique)
3. Frantz Fanon (Martinique)
4. Léon Gontran Damas (French Guiana)
5. Jacques Roumain (Haiti)
Negritude's legacy:
1. Inspired African and Caribbean writers to explore their cultural identities
2. Influenced the development of African literature and postcolonial studies
3. Contributed to the global fight against colonialism and racism
4. Shaped the Black Arts Movement in the United States
5. Continues to inspire contemporary debates on identity, culture, and social justice.
Conclusion:
Negritude's impact extends beyond literature to art, music, and politics, making it a significant cultural and intellectual movement of the 20th century.
To be continued
From Ifybeckdiv Global Tv (Education, Literary and Language Hub)



Chad Gard, if I am understanding you correctly, you are saying that he wrote checks, or his business/legal team wrote checks, in 2017, and that labeling what clearly look to be legal expenses, as legal expenses, amounted to “falsifying business records,” even though the records are right there — for everyone to see — and they are not “falsified.” The expenses actually happened, and the payments were actually made. 

“Falsifying” business records, for example, is what corrupt politicians do. They get millions to, for example, build something - and they submit all kinds of false records to make it look like that something was built — and then either that something never gets built at all — or a lesser version of the something gets built, photographed, and abandoned. The falsified business records in that case would be a pile of bills paid to contractors, materials purchased — fake names — shell companies — and those contractors do not exist as people. The materials were never purchased. The money is then shuffled around, and if it can be traced, sometimes, the perpetrators go to jail. There’s a pile of fake bills, receipts, payments, etc. 

In Trump’s case — the expenses not only went to the people mentioned, but the purpose is also correct. There are no “fake companies” that received money. The correct people are cited, and the correct purpose is cited. Where is the crime?

Maybe let’s try with a few clear examples…

To use the example of stealing a car, to “not” have committed the crime, the thief would simply need to have not stolen the car. 

In Trump’s case: what is the thing that he did, that was a crime, that had he not done, he would not be a criminal? Also: how should he have labeled those checks then?

Someone claiming that this case proves that Trump is a criminal must be able to take all of the “elements” of the case — and rearrange the elements — so that no crime would have been committed. Can you do that? 

Let’s consider not only theft (where simply: not stealing would then not be a crime), let’s also consider arson. 

In the theft of a car, the thief would have needed to have not stolen the car — then there would have been no crime. To make “arson” into “not arson,” then the fire needs to never have been set. If there was no intentionally set fire — then there could not have been arson. 

Are you following?

You would have to be able to show a “non-crime” version of Trump’s behavior, if you’re claiming that he committed a crime. 

Now, you’re claiming that somehow, these invoices, entries, and checks “prove” that Trump falsified business records. How? How do these checks prove Trump falsified any business records?

Let’s grab an example:

“11
Guilty
Invoice from Michael Cohen, marked as a record of Donald J. Trump	
May 22, 2017”

That’s an invoice. How does that specific invoice prove the crime Donald Trump was convicted of?

Next, this alleged falsification, which happened in 2017, somehow proves that Trump not only conspired to influence an election, but that he hid election interference?

WHAT?

Don’t you think a felony should be clear and understandable — not a long string of assumptions and claims where every step of the way, the claims don’t make any sense?

Shouldn’t you be able to clearly explain what the crime even was — and also — shouldn’t you be able to explain what Trump would have needed to have done, so that these checks would not be: 

1) falsifying business records in 2017, that
2) supposedly proves that he intentionally hid his 
3) 2016 election interference 

and at the end of it…somehow all of this has to do with “sex with a porn star?” 

So?

Please put the “elements” of this case into a sequence that a) makes Trump into a criminal and b) would have made Trump into “not a criminal.”

Let them ignore you.
Let them be "right."
Let them doubt you.
Let them not like you.
Let them not speak to you.
Let them run your name in the ground.
Let them make you out to be the villain.
Whatever it is that people want to say about you, let them! 
Kindly step aside and LET THEM.
The hard truth is they know how much they are hurting you. They just simply don't care. They did it knowing it could cause them to lose you. They did it anyway.  People that love you care about how they make you feel. 
The end. 
Let them go. 
There will be people that would rather lose you than be honest about what they've done to you. Let them go.
The lack of respect was the closure.  The lack of apology was the closure.  The lack of care was the closure. The lack of acountability was the closure. The lack of honestly was the closure.  Let them go. 
Make the decision to no longer sit at tables where you might be the topic when you get up. Let them go. 
You can still be kind. You can even still love them deeply. But do it from the distance they created in their words and actions. Access to you is a privilege they have proven they can’t be trusted with. Let them go. 
You don’t need to tell your side of the story. God already knows. Let God fight the battle for you. Let them go. 
It’s taken me a long time to get here. Sleepless nights, countless tears, managing a range of emotions filled with anger, disappointment, confusion and deep hurt.  Lots of self reflection, self preservation, deep prayer and seeking wisdom from those much wiser than me.  
If you are struggling with this please know you are not alone.  We will never understand why hurt people hurt people. But we can do the hard work to grow ourselves.  Because healed people do in fact heal people. 
Don’t you dare let them steal your joy. 
Don’t you dare let them steal your light. 
Don’t you dare let them steal your peace. 
You are in control of that. 
Hold tight to what you can control and release your grip on what you can’t control.
Let them go.

When dealing with narcissism, you should know that it's not personal. "It isn't personal" is one of those cliches used to cushion all kinds of bad actions taken by people who need an out for being immoral, but in this case it actually gets near the truth. Narcissists don't know how to love or be a friend; they can't afford to spare the energy to learn, because they're always in a state of high emergency, cataloging potential threats and redoubling their defenses. When they claim to love you, it means nothing. They may even think they mean it, but they don't understand the concept - they can't feel it. They never attach to you or anyone else. Other people are paper cut-outs to the narcissist, like those cardboard figures of celebrities you pose next to for a selfie. Narcissist value their own children only as mirrors of themselves. When they destabilize you or attack you, it means nothing. They are stuck in an endless conversation with themselves, in which you are an inanimate object, to be assigned their own faults and used as a surrogate punching bag for their hatred of themselves. When they toss you out, it's no more meaningful than a junkie tossing away a needle; when they try to reel you back in, it only means that they tired of the new drug and need a hit of the old. None of this is personal. They're too terrified to have personal relationships, opting instead for extraction of admiration from a subservient partner whose range of action they strictly constrain. This is not personal. None of it. The narcissist does not know who you are. it doesn't know how to know other people. Like the vampire or the chainsaw-wielding creature in the horror film, it's from another world, bereft of the concept of human connection. Moreover, People wonder why they end up hurt, seriously hurt, and even killed for their own actions. Cheating is a choice and there's simply a lot of ignorance in the process....

“1. When I came to you with my idea for a BLM glove, you wanted to do  Go Fund Me campaign to raise $30K. “


That’s not true. 


“I felt that was unethical because I didn’t need startup money due to my relationship with the manufacturer.”

Generating pre-sales would not have been unethical. It was Kickstarter, and I still have the files. 


“Instead of honoring my wishes, you wanted take my idea and do it on your own. I found that to be hurtful, insensitive, and disrespectful.”

That’s ridiculous, I never wanted to take the idea and do it on my own. If I had “wanted” to do that — I would have done it. 


“You eventually apologized and let the matter go, but you made it clear that you felt I cost us some money.”

What you “cost” us is the chance to make a bit of money, yes. 

“However, I spoke with a few attorney friends of mine who agreed that an unnecessary Go Fund Me would have been unethical. This was the first strain on our friendship.”

Bill, it was a Kickstarter, and I sensed that we had a fairly short time window, and I was right. BLM has descended into allegations of fraud, scam, corruption etc etc. I didn’t know what exactly was going to happen with BLM, but I did correctly assess that we had a short time window. 

We would have taken pre-orders. Your insistence that taking pre-orders is unethical is just not rational. Go to kickstarter — I have purchased several innovative things before product release from kickstarter. It’s lost its initial “coolness” now, but at the time, it was a cool concept, they were promoting BLM products for free, and your concept would have actually come to life, had you just said “yes,” to doing a kickstarter. 

I made the pre-kickstarter, and all you would have needed to do is say “yes,” and the campaign would have launched. If Kickstarters don’t make enough money, they return the money and the campaign is considered “unscuccessful.”

We agreed that no one in your circle would find out about my skin tone. What happened after you told them my skin tone? Everything that came from me was suppressed, not allowed, considered “unethical” etc etc, well OK, instead of sticking to what was happening — and instead of keeping yourself from getting played — you let them convince you to distance yourself from me — because of the color of my skin and how your “friends” treated you because of the color of my skin. 

The BLMgloves project ended, because you told the BLM people that I’m white. 

If “you were right,” then the gloves would be a part of the BLM line-up, and they would have had visibility in the marches, movement, media, etc. They didn’t. You also got played and that has continued to be a source of frustration for me. Your “friend” Marvin is some bigshot millionaire — but you were on unemployment. That really messes with me, Bill. The idea was that we were going to help each other and support each other until we “made it,” and that means millions. 

Would I let you stay on unemployment, if I “made it big,” and received some kind of big up-front money for one of my movie ideas, like this one: https://dainis.net/ideas/movie-idea-the-chicago-five/

Bill, prior to these situations, I clearly would have gotten you on board as a creative on the team. 

Now what?

Did you have anyone backing you to the point of putting aside paid projects and working for you for free? 

No, they ripped you off, took advantage of you, and didn’t let you even do a Kickstarter to get some presales for YOUR idea?

I backed you and your idea fully. I put myself behind it and invested time effort skill equipment etc. Where there is love, friendship — I have done truly miraculous things — and clearly I don’t know how to “design gloves,” but I did for you — and the materials were good enough to get some sales. 

You’d be “right” in this matter, if you had even just a few thousand sales — but you don’t. Your wondeful idea is now buried — and you had a very brief shot. 

A few clicks, and at least the idea would have had a chance on Kickstarter — and Kickstarter campaigns are NOT unethical.

5. No matter how attractive your body is or how hot the lingerie you wear, a man is turned on most by your attitude.
6. Men also love it when the wife makes romantic advances. Don't be passive, letting him do all the work. Take your husband out on dates, seduce him, flirt with him, show him that you find him attractive.

In Ancient Greece, Socrates had a great reputation for wisdom. One day, someone came to find the great philosopher and said to him:
"Do you know what I just heard about your friend?"
"A moment," replied Socrates. "Before you tell me, I would like to test it with the three sieves."
"The three sieves?"
"Yes," continued Socrates. "Before you speak about others, it's important to take the time to filter what you mean. I call it the test of the three sieves. The first sieve is TRUTH. Have you checked if what you're going to tell me is true?"
"No, I just heard it."
"Very well! So, you don't know if it's true. Let's move on to the second sieve, that of KINDNESS. Is what you want to tell me about my friend something good?"
"Oh, no! On the contrary."
"So," questioned Socrates, "you want to tell me something negative about him, and you're not even sure it's true? Perhaps you can still pass the test of the third sieve, that of UTILITY. Is it useful for me to know what you're going to tell me about this friend?"
"No, not really."
"Therefore," concluded Socrates, "what you were going to tell me is neither true, nor good, nor useful. Why, then, did you want to tell me this?"
"Gossip is a bad thing. Initially, it may seem enjoyable and fun, but ultimately, it fills our hearts with bitterness and poisons us." - Pope Francis

Dear Modern Musician Family!

Hi, my name is Dainis W. Michel. I am feeling very shy about introducing myself here. I will share a bit of back-story after I share some links

This is a “score bookshelf” at my website
https://dainis.net/music/score-bookshelf/
though it is incomplete.

A nice pop song of mine is available here: https://open.spotify.com/track/5FdMr6pnCN3ZuZbkhRV4pC?si=1f2e921360ce475b

I recently entered a song competition with these two songs, and if you like them, pressing “like” would be very much appreciated. Last year, I won the “audience favorite” award (which was based on likes), so that was quite nice. 

https://fb.watch/sZahuvQf4z/

https://fb.watch/sZai4OxncQ/

A short comment like “wonderful!” or “skaisti” or “brīnišķīgi!” would be greatly appreciated!

I’ve written a few books, including one on songwriting: https://dainis.net/learn-how-to-write-your-songs-down

My students have done very very well, but I am scared that sharing that aspect of my life could be interpreted as some kind of self-marketing to the group — for which I could be reprimanded and my posts could be removed, etc. 

My back-story is that my xWife promised to “sell me,” and I promised to sell her (as a singer). I did my part, but she did not do hers. As a result, I have been able to win awards with my music, but I have basically sold nothing at all. Like nothing. Or almost completely nothing. 

I am a good teacher, but presenting myself as such, for example in FB groups, has met with severe severe backlash. 

I had done all of the coursework and just had my dissertation to write — and I would have a doctorate in Musikwissenschaft from the University of Vienna — but I spent 10 years as a FT single dad, after which my daughter was abducted. 

That kind stress kept me from completing my doctorate, which is why I am not currently a music composition professor…which was my life-plan. 

I teach privately and do stuff like this from time to time: 
https://www.tiktok.com/@dainisw.michel/video/7335666059145530657

https://www.tiktok.com/@dainisw.michel/video/7346977284416425248

https://www.tiktok.com/@dainisw.michel/video/7222371820383620378

I would say about 1million Latvians know me as a public personality and musician, and I gave a fairly successful concert last year on the 4th of July. 

I struggle deeply with the betrayal I’ve faced with regard to my xWife promising to “sell me,” regarding selling my compositions (sync placements, media, movies, commercials), because I knew/know that I am just so utterly terrible at “selling myself,” and I don’t exactly know how to turn the corner on that. 

Even though the “rules” of this server don’t appear before we introduce ourselves, I’m concerned that sharing the link to the book I’ve written about songwriting will be construed as “pitching” to the group. I haven’t even sold one copy of that eBook this year. The testimonials are real — I wrote a recommendation for one of my former students to get a teaching job this year — but “selling eBooks about songwriting” was something that happened naturally over 10 years ago. Now, it looks like the social media environment is pay to play — only — and people are just so incredibly cruel about anyone even trying to earn a living through anything other than paid ads. 

So, if I am going to be berated here for presenting myself, then I guess that’s what is going to happen. 

I am a very helpful person and am unfortunately in the position of having over over over over over “paid it forward,” with very little in return. 

I have a few “offers” I actually could make for the group, but at the moment, I am incredibly tired. I’ve regained contact with my daughter and after now 3 more years of ridiculous defending myself against the impossibly insane law in Austria that: if a mother says it, it is considered true and legally binding, and if a father claims something else is true, he has to prove it…I mean I just “won” in court, but my daughter is now 17. It’s been an incredibly fatiguing journey. 

Ideally, if I can figure out some way to use “street team,” and I can also shake off the sadness and fatigue that I feel, I could have a “Starter Kit” pre-sales page ready by Sunday, because on that day, I am participating in a family camp where I’ve sung almost every year for the last few years. Pre-abduction, my daughter and I are singing at that camp here: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=lw6xfVZ2LO0

I have paid for 4 months already and have hesitated to start, in part because of my fear of being berated or reprimanded for just presenting myself as who I am — which includes being an author, solfeggio, composition, arranging and songwriting teacher. 

Maybe I will be welcomed at Modern Musician as I am…we’ll see.

Vēlos pateikties, par skaistajiem brīžiem, kad biju aicināts…man ļoti patikās talkot un justies piederīgam. Bija itsevišķi skaisti pasniegt un izveidot jaunas dziesmas.

Iekopēšu šeit audio ierakstu, kuru ierakstīju šī gada maijā, un mazliet ieklausoties, ierakstā dalos ar pārkāpumiem, kuriem tieša sakara ar Pērlēm nav…bet nespēšu vēlreiz kko šādu ierakstīt…tātad atstāšu. 

(Ieraksts)

Vēlos arī pateikt: ja saņēmēji pirms rudens noklausīsies un atbildēs, pateikšos. Steigas nav. 

Kopš ieraksta, pēdīgi, Austrijas tiesā varēju saņemt patiesu lēmumu sakarā ar Emītes situāciju…bet arī sanāk tā, ka Pērles ļaudis gan nejuta situācijai līdzi, un izpalīdzīgu atbalstu nesniedza.

2022. g. vasarā sagatavoju dzejas, dziesmas, uzdevumus, ievingrināju eiritmiju…domādams, ka protams mūsu sadarbība turpināsies. Bet mani neņēma kā skolotāju. Man pateica es varot droši nākt ciemoties. Bet es taču negribēju tikai “ciemoties.” Es būtu daudz uzņēmies, lai būtu Pērlēs pasniedzēja/skolotāja lomā, lai izveidotu kvalitatīvu mācību programmu, lai visu finansētu, un lai mūsu sadarbība būtu savstarpēji atbalstoša un skaista. 

Jutos patiesi “saukts,” kad Jānis Vītols man pateica, ka viņš priecātos, ja mūsu kopēji izveidotās dziesmas tiktu ierakstītas, un 2023. gada martā, Rasa man piezvanīja un pateica, ka tās ierakstīsim pēc dziesmu svētkiem…ka mani lūgs uz Pērlēm, un to svēto darbiņu paveiksim…

Bet tas nenotikās un tagad vairāk nekā gadu, neesmu itin nekā no Pērlēm dzirdējis…izņemot Rotas lūgumu mājiņu pieskatīt…ar kuru es sāku pārdomāt manas pamata vērtības sakarā ar draugiem un kopienām un manu līdzdalību gan draudzībās gan kopienās. 

Es pieņemu, ka būtu varējis vienkārši ierasties. Dot no sevīm. Strādāt. Bet vai mums ir abpusēji atbalstoša un atgrezeniski labvēlīga sadarbība un izpalīdzīga iesaiste viens otra ikdienās?

Christine Decroix on Michael  (KLAVIERES!)

"As a friend, I spent a great amount of time in the recording studio with him, we always had children with us and were always laughing and playing between recording sessions. He brought a lot of joy in people lives. I grew up in Belgium raised by my dad who, as a chief of police, taught me to always be suspicious and I can tell you that I couldn’t see anything wrong with Michael, except maybe that it was a man who at a young age never had the time to be a kid. He told me once that children are pure and innocent and adults always want something from him. That’s the sole reason he felt more comfortable with children, they just loved him because he was magic for the kids and made them feel like giants. He loathed vulgarity and would have been upset at me laughing with a dirty joke in the studio.
He built a movie theatre for disabled children in his house. People are sick to think he did that to attract them as a child molester. They judge without knowing and should be ashamed because they largely contributed to his downfall and his death. Michael Jackson was hypersensitive, maybe it was the key of his huge talent. He suffered tremendously of all these false accusations and the slanders that were spread. These unscrupulous persons took everything away from him, including his amazing career.
He was a genius and an amazing talent already at a young age. Nobody can judge him without knowing him. If one of you had spent only one hour with him, you would have fallen in love with his pure heart. He could make everybody around him feel special. He was even thanking you for working with him, and had definitely not a big star attitude, he was down to earth, lived on a healthy diet, never drank alcohol. The day of my birthday party in Tokyo he took my glass of champagne away from me and replaced it by a glass of water. He was not joking he just cared for people.
I know today that his place belongs in Paradise.

KLAVIERES

June 21st, 2015:
Not everyone you meet will give you the respect or love that you deserve. Respect them anyway. Love them anyway. No matter what you do, be kind. It is better to be kind and hurt, than unkind and cause pain. You were given the gift of gentleness and kindness. You were given the gift of a soft heart. So do not lose it. Do not allow your heart to harden. Just because someone caused you pain, it does not mean that everyone will. Just because someone betrayed your trust, it does not mean that others aren't trustworthy. Just because someone broke your heart, it does not mean that it will remain broken forever. It is better to love with a whole heart, to give with a whole heart, and to trust with a whole heart, than to never experience the beauty of love, the reward of giving, and the comfort of trusting. And when you fall hard, you can choose to remain on the ground for as long as you want, but you can also choose to get back up. Love again. Give again. Trust again. It is the experience that grows you, not the fear of it.


Steph Magenta
